CStrings:
+ "\n\nconstant constexpr int QCCE_THREADS = 128;\nconstant constexpr int QCCE_NUM_SGS = 4;\nconstant constexpr int QCCE_MAX_GROUPS = 64;  // upper bound on D / GS\n\ntemplate <typename T, int GS, int BM, int BITS>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_forward(\n    const device T*        x            [[buffer(0)]],\n    const device uint32_t* w_packed     [[buffer(1)]],\n    const device T*        scales       [[buffer(2)]],\n    const device T*        biases       [[buffer(3)]],\n    const device int32_t*  targets      [[buffer(4)]],\n    device float*          lse_out      [[buffer(5)]],\n    device float*          loss_per_row [[buffer(6)]],\n    const constant int&    M            [[buffer(7)]],\n    const constant int&    D            [[buffer(8)]],\n    const constant int&    V            [[buffer(9)]],\n    threadgroup T*         x_tile       [[threadgroup(0)]],\n    uint                   gid          [[threadgroup_position_in_grid]],\n    uint                   tid          [[thread_position_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   lane         [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]],\n    uint                   sg_id        [[simdgroup_index_in_threadgroup]]) {\n  const int m_base = int(gid) * BM;\n  if (m_base >= M) return;\n\n  constexpr int EL_PER_PACK = 32 / BITS;       // 8 for bits=4, 4 for bits=8\n  const int num_groups   = D / GS;\n  const int packs_per_row = D / EL_PER_PACK;\n  const int packs_per_grp = GS / EL_PER_PACK;\n\n  threadgroup int   tg_target[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_target_logit[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_sg_max[BM][QCCE_NUM_SGS];\n  threadgroup float tg_sg_sum[BM][QCCE_NUM_SGS];\n  threadgroup float x_sum_tg[BM][QCCE_MAX_GROUPS];\n\n  // Cooperative load: x[m_base..m_base+BM, :] -> x_tile[BM*D]\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * D; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / D;\n    const int k = idx - r * D;\n    x_tile[r * D + k] = x[(m_base + r) * D + k];\n  }\n  if (tid < BM) {\n    tg_target[tid] = targets[m_base + tid];\n    tg_target_logit[tid] = 0.0f;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Precompute x_sum[r][g] = sum over k in group g of x_tile[r, k].\n  // Each thread handles one (r, g) — only first BM*num_groups threads do work.\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * num_groups; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / num_groups;\n    const int g = idx - r * num_groups;\n    float xs = 0.0f;\n    const int k_start = g * GS;\n    for (int k = 0; k < GS; k++) {\n      xs += float(x_tile[r * D + k_start + k]);\n    }\n    x_sum_tg[r][g] = xs;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Per-thread, per-row online LSE state — all threads track identical values\n  // (they consume the same TG-broadcast m_tile/s_tile per iteration).\n  float m_running[BM];\n  float s_running[BM];\n  for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n    m_running[r] = -INFINITY;\n    s_running[r] = 0.0f;\n  }\n\n  const int num_tiles = (V + QCCE_THREADS - 1) / QCCE_THREADS;\n  for (int tile = 0; tile < num_tiles; tile++) {\n    const int v = tile * QCCE_THREADS + int(tid);\n    float logit[BM];\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = -INFINITY;\n\n    if (v < V) {\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = 0.0f;\n      const device uint32_t* w_row = w_packed + v * packs_per_row;\n      const device T* s_row_p = scales + v * num_groups;\n      const device T* b_row_p = biases + v * num_groups;\n\n      for (int g = 0; g < num_groups; g++) {\n        float s = float(s_row_p[g]);\n        float b = float(b_row_p[g]);\n        float qx_sum[BM];\n        for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) qx_sum[r] = 0.0f;\n        const int k0_g = g * GS;\n        for (int p = 0; p < packs_per_grp; p++) {\n          const int k0 = k0_g + p * EL_PER_PACK;\n          uint32_t packed = w_row[k0 / EL_PER_PACK];  // shared across BM rows\n          float qs[EL_PER_PACK];\n          if constexpr (BITS == 4) {\n            for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n              uint8_t byte = (packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff;\n              qs[byte_idx * 2]     = float(byte & 0x0f);\n              qs[byte_idx * 2 + 1] = float((byte >> 4) & 0x0f);\n            }\n          } else {  // BITS == 8\n            for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n              qs[byte_idx] = float((packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff);\n            }\n          }\n          for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n            for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n              qx_sum[r] += qs[i] * float(x_tile[r * D + k0 + i]);\n            }\n          }\n        }\n        for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n          logit[r] += s * qx_sum[r] + b * x_sum_tg[r][g];\n        }\n      }\n\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n        if (v == tg_target[r]) tg_target_logit[r] = logit[r];\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Per-row TG-wide max via 4-SG partial reduction.\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float sg_max = simd_max(logit[r]);\n      if (lane == 0) tg_sg_max[r][sg_id] = sg_max;\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    float new_m[BM];\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float m_tile = max(max(tg_sg_max[r][0], tg_sg_max[r][1]),\n                         max(tg_sg_max[r][2], tg_sg_max[r][3]));\n      new_m[r] = max(m_running[r], m_tile);\n    }\n\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float exp_term = (logit[r] > -INFINITY) ? metal::fast::exp(logit[r] - new_m[r]) : 0.0f;\n      float sg_sum = simd_sum(exp_term);\n      if (lane == 0) tg_sg_sum[r][sg_id] = sg_sum;\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float s_tile = tg_sg_sum[r][0] + tg_sg_sum[r][1] + tg_sg_sum[r][2] + tg_sg_sum[r][3];\n      float scale_old = (m_running[r] > -INFINITY) ? metal::fast::exp(m_running[r] - new_m[r]) : 0.0f;\n      s_running[r] = s_running[r] * scale_old + s_tile;\n      m_running[r] = new_m[r];\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (tid < BM) {\n    float lse = metal::fast::log(s_running[tid]) + m_running[tid];\n    lse_out[m_base + tid] = lse;\n    loss_per_row[m_base + tid] = lse - tg_target_logit[tid];\n  }\n}\n\n// Mean reduction: loss = mean(loss_per_row). One TG, 32 lanes (M is small).\ntemplate <typename T>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_loss_reduce(\n    const device float* loss_per_row [[buffer(0)]],\n    device T*           loss_out     [[buffer(1)]],\n    const constant int& M            [[buffer(2)]],\n    uint                lane         [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]]) {\n  float sum = 0.0f;\n  for (int i = int(lane); i < M; i += 32) {\n    sum += loss_per_row[i];\n  }\n  sum = simd_sum(sum);\n  if (lane == 0) {\n    loss_out[0] = T(sum / float(M));\n  }\n}\n\n// Backward: d_x[m, k] = sum_v (softmax[m, v] - 1{v==target[m]}) * cot/M * W[v, k]\n//\n// Two-phase per V-tile (128 v's per tile):\n//   Phase 1 (tid = v offset): recompute logit per row, derive d_logit per row,\n//     store in d_logit_tile[BM][128].\n//   Phase 2 (tid = k_chunk index): for each of 128 v's in this tile, dequant 8\n//     W values once and FMA into accum[BM][8]; flush into d_x_acc[BM][D]. The\n//     per-TG fp32 accumulator is private to the TG.\n//\n// Grid: (M/BM, V/128, 1) — qmm-style tiling. Each TG handles BM rows × one\n// 128-v tile. Many small TGs keep all GPU cores busy. At end, the per-TG\n// d_x_acc[BM, D] is atomic_fetch_add'd into d_x_acc_global[M, D] fp32.\n// Caller must zero d_x_acc_global before dispatching this kernel.\ntemplate <typename T, int GS, int BM, int BITS>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_backward(\n    const device T*        cot            [[buffer(0)]],\n    const device T*        x              [[buffer(1)]],\n    const device uint32_t* w_packed       [[buffer(2)]],\n    const device T*        scales         [[buffer(3)]],\n    const device T*        biases         [[buffer(4)]],\n    const device int32_t*  targets        [[buffer(5)]],\n    const device float*    lse            [[buffer(6)]],\n    device atomic_float*   d_x_acc_global [[buffer(7)]],\n    const constant int&    M              [[buffer(8)]],\n    const constant int&    D              [[buffer(9)]],\n    const constant int&    V              [[buffer(10)]],\n    threadgroup T*         x_tile         [[threadgroup(0)]],\n    threadgroup float*     d_x_acc        [[threadgroup(1)]],\n    uint2                  gid            [[threadgroup_position_in_grid]],\n    uint2                  tid_v          [[thread_position_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   lane           [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]],\n    uint                   sg_id          [[simdgroup_index_in_threadgroup]]) {\n  const uint tid = tid_v.x;\n  const int m_base = int(gid.x) * BM;\n  if (m_base >= M) return;\n  const int v_base = int(gid.y) * QCCE_THREADS;\n  if (v_base >= V) return;\n\n  constexpr int EL_PER_PACK = 32 / BITS;\n  const int num_groups   = D / GS;\n  const int packs_per_row = D / EL_PER_PACK;\n  const int packs_per_grp = GS / EL_PER_PACK;\n\n  threadgroup int   tg_target[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_lse[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_cot_over_M;\n  threadgroup float d_logit_tile[BM][QCCE_THREADS];\n  threadgroup float x_sum_tg[BM][QCCE_MAX_GROUPS];\n\n  // Cooperative load: x rows -> x_tile, zero TG-local d_x_acc.\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * D; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / D;\n    const int k = idx - r * D;\n    x_tile[r * D + k] = x[(m_base + r) * D + k];\n    d_x_acc[r * D + k] = 0.0f;\n  }\n  if (tid < BM) {\n    tg_target[tid] = targets[m_base + tid];\n    tg_lse[tid]    = lse[m_base + tid];\n  }\n  if (tid == 0) {\n    tg_cot_over_M = float(cot[0]) / float(M);\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Precompute x_sum[r][g] = sum over k in group g of x_tile[r, k].\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * num_groups; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / num_groups;\n    const int g = idx - r * num_groups;\n    float xs = 0.0f;\n    const int k_start = g * GS;\n    for (int k = 0; k < GS; k++) {\n      xs += float(x_tile[r * D + k_start + k]);\n    }\n    x_sum_tg[r][g] = xs;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Single 128-v tile per TG: tid = v offset within tile.\n  const int v = v_base + int(tid);\n\n  // Phase 1: recompute logit per row for this thread's v.\n  float logit[BM];\n  for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = -INFINITY;\n\n  if (v < V) {\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = 0.0f;\n    const device uint32_t* w_row = w_packed + v * packs_per_row;\n    const device T* s_row_p = scales + v * num_groups;\n    const device T* b_row_p = biases + v * num_groups;\n\n    for (int g = 0; g < num_groups; g++) {\n      float s = float(s_row_p[g]);\n      float b = float(b_row_p[g]);\n      float qx_sum[BM];\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) qx_sum[r] = 0.0f;\n      const int k0_g = g * GS;\n      for (int p = 0; p < packs_per_grp; p++) {\n        const int k0 = k0_g + p * EL_PER_PACK;\n        uint32_t packed = w_row[k0 / EL_PER_PACK];\n        float qs[EL_PER_PACK];\n        if constexpr (BITS == 4) {\n          for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n            uint8_t byte = (packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff;\n            qs[byte_idx * 2]     = float(byte & 0x0f);\n            qs[byte_idx * 2 + 1] = float((byte >> 4) & 0x0f);\n          }\n        } else {  // BITS == 8\n          for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n            qs[byte_idx] = float((packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff);\n          }\n        }\n        for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n          for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n            qx_sum[r] += qs[i] * float(x_tile[r * D + k0 + i]);\n          }\n        }\n      }\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n        logit[r] += s * qx_sum[r] + b * x_sum_tg[r][g];\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n    float p_val = 0.0f;\n    if (v < V) {\n      p_val = metal::fast::exp(logit[r] - tg_lse[r]);\n      if (v == tg_target[r]) p_val -= 1.0f;\n    }\n    d_logit_tile[r][tid] = p_val * tg_cot_over_M;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Phase 2: each thread handles k_chunks, accumulates over all 128 v's of\n  // this tile. W reads are shared across BM rows.\n  for (int k_chunk = int(tid); k_chunk < packs_per_row; k_chunk += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int k0 = k_chunk * EL_PER_PACK;\n    const int g  = k0 / GS;\n    float accum[BM][EL_PER_PACK];\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) accum[r][i] = 0.0f;\n    }\n\n    for (int vi = 0; vi < QCCE_THREADS; vi++) {\n      const int v_global = v_base + vi;\n      if (v_global >= V) break;\n      uint32_t packed = w_packed[v_global * packs_per_row + k_chunk];\n      float s = float(scales[v_global * num_groups + g]);\n      float b = float(biases[v_global * num_groups + g]);\n      float qs[EL_PER_PACK];\n      if constexpr (BITS == 4) {\n        for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n          uint8_t byte = (packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff;\n          qs[byte_idx * 2]     = float(byte & 0x0f);\n          qs[byte_idx * 2 + 1] = float((byte >> 4) & 0x0f);\n        }\n      } else {  // BITS == 8\n        for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n          qs[byte_idx] = float((packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff);\n        }\n      }\n      for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n        float w_i = s * qs[i] + b;\n        for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n          float dl = d_logit_tile[r][vi];\n          accum[r][i] += dl * w_i;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n        d_x_acc[r * D + k0 + i] = accum[r][i];\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Atomic flush: add this TG's partial d_x to global. Each TG owns a unique\n  // (m_block, v_block) pair; multiple v_blocks contribute to same d_x[m, k],\n  // so atomic_fetch_add is required for cross-TG accumulation.\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * D; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / D;\n    const int k = idx - r * D;\n    atomic_fetch_add_explicit(\n        &d_x_acc_global[(m_base + r) * D + k],\n        d_x_acc[r * D + k],\n        memory_order_relaxed);\n  }\n}\n\n// Zero a fp32 buffer. One thread per element. Caller dispatches with N total\n// threads to clear d_x_acc_global before the atomic-accumulating backward.\n[[kernel]] void qcce_zero_fp32(\n    device float*       buf [[buffer(0)]],\n    const constant int& N   [[buffer(1)]],\n    uint                gid [[thread_position_in_grid]]) {\n  if (int(gid) >= N) return;\n  buf[gid] = 0.0f;\n}\n\n// Cast the fp32 chunk-accumulated d_x into the final T-typed d_x output.\n// One thread per element; total threads = M * D.\ntemplate <typename T>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_backward_finalize(\n    const device float* d_x_acc_global [[buffer(0)]],\n    device T*           d_x            [[buffer(1)]],\n    const constant int& N              [[buffer(2)]],\n    uint                gid            [[thread_position_in_grid]]) {\n  if (int(gid) >= N) return;\n  d_x[gid] = T(d_x_acc_global[gid]);\n}\n\n"
+ "\n\ntemplate <\n    typename T,\n    int GS,\n    int BITS,\n    int BM,\n    int BN,\n    int BK,\n    int WM,\n    int WN,\n    bool aligned_M>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_forward_steel(\n    const device T*        x            [[buffer(0)]],\n    const device uint32_t* w_packed     [[buffer(1)]],\n    const device T*        scales       [[buffer(2)]],\n    const device T*        biases       [[buffer(3)]],\n    const device int32_t*  targets      [[buffer(4)]],\n    device float*          partials     [[buffer(5)]],\n    const constant int&    M            [[buffer(6)]],\n    const constant int&    D            [[buffer(7)]],\n    const constant int&    V            [[buffer(8)]],\n    const constant int&    V_slab       [[buffer(9)]],\n    uint3                  tid          [[threadgroup_position_in_grid]],\n    uint                   lid          [[thread_index_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   sg_id        [[simdgroup_index_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   lane         [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]]) {\n  constexpr int tgp_size = WM * WN * 32;\n  constexpr int BK_padded = BK + 16 / sizeof(T);\n  constexpr int PACK = 32 / BITS;\n  constexpr int BPP = 4;  // bytes_per_pack: uint32 -> 4 bytes\n\n  threadgroup T     Xs[BM * BK_padded];\n  threadgroup T     Ws[BN * BK_padded];\n  threadgroup float logits_tile[BM * BN];\n  threadgroup float m_running[BM];\n  threadgroup float s_running[BM];\n  threadgroup float target_logit[BM];\n  threadgroup int   tg_target[BM];\n\n  const int m_base = int(tid.x) * BM;\n  if (m_base >= M) return;\n  const int m_actual = aligned_M ? BM : min(BM, M - m_base);\n  const int v_slab_start = int(tid.y) * V_slab;\n  if (v_slab_start >= V) return;\n  const int v_slab_end = min(v_slab_start + V_slab, V);\n\n  if (lid < uint(BM)) {\n    m_running[lid]     = -INFINITY;\n    s_running[lid]     = 0.0f;\n    target_logit[lid]  = 0.0f;\n    tg_target[lid]     = (int(lid) < m_actual) ? targets[m_base + lid] : -1;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  using mma_t = mlx::steel::BlockMMA<\n      T, T, BM, BN, BK, WM, WN, false, true, BK_padded, BK_padded>;\n  using loader_x_t = mlx::steel::BlockLoader<\n      T, BM, BK, BK_padded, 1, tgp_size>;\n  using loader_w_t = QuantizedBlockLoader<\n      T, BN, BK, BK_padded, 1, tgp_size, GS, BITS>;\n\n  const int K_w = D * BPP / PACK;\n  const int K_g = D / GS;\n\n  for (int v_tile = v_slab_start; v_tile < v_slab_end; v_tile += BN) {\n    const device T* x_ptr = x + m_base * (int64_t)D;\n    const device uint8_t* w_ptr =\n        ((const device uint8_t*)w_packed) + v_tile * (int64_t)K_w;\n    const device T* s_ptr = scales + v_tile * (int64_t)K_g;\n    const device T* b_ptr = biases + v_tile * (int64_t)K_g;\n\n    loader_x_t loader_x(x_ptr, D, Xs, sg_id, lane);\n    loader_w_t loader_w(w_ptr, s_ptr, b_ptr, D, Ws, sg_id, lane);\n    mma_t mma_op(sg_id, lane);\n    mma_op.Ctile.clear();\n\n    for (int k = 0; k < D; k += BK) {\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n      if (aligned_M) {\n        loader_x.load_unsafe();\n      } else {\n        loader_x.load_safe(short2(BK, m_actual));\n      }\n      loader_w.load_unsafe();\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n      mma_op.mma(Xs, Ws);\n      loader_x.next();\n      loader_w.next();\n    }\n\n    // Ctile (fp32, BM×BN) -> logits_tile in TG memory, row-major.\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n    mma_op.Ctile.template store<float, WM, WN, BN, 1>(\n        logits_tile + mma_op.sm * BN + mma_op.sn);\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    // Per-row online-LSE reduction. BM rows split evenly across WM*WN SGs;\n    // each SG handles ROWS_PER_SG rows sequentially. Within a row, the SG's\n    // 32 lanes hold its BN=32 logits, reduced via simd_max / simd_sum.\n    constexpr int ROWS_PER_SG = BM / (WM * WN);\n    STEEL_PRAGMA_UNROLL\n    for (int rr = 0; rr < ROWS_PER_SG; rr++) {\n      int row = int(sg_id) * ROWS_PER_SG + rr;\n      float logit = logits_tile[row * BN + int(lane)];\n      int v_global = v_tile + int(lane);\n      if (v_global == tg_target[row]) {\n        target_logit[row] = logit;\n      }\n      float m_tile = simd_max(logit);\n      float m_new  = max(m_running[row], m_tile);\n      float e      = metal::fast::exp(logit - m_new);\n      float s_tile = simd_sum(e);\n      if (lane == 0) {\n        float scale_old = (m_running[row] > -INFINITY)\n            ? metal::fast::exp(m_running[row] - m_new)\n            : 0.0f;\n        s_running[row] = s_running[row] * scale_old + s_tile;\n        m_running[row] = m_new;\n      }\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n  }\n\n  // Emit partials[v_block, m_base+r, 0..2] for this (m_block, v_block).\n  if (lid < uint(BM)) {\n    int row = int(lid);\n    if (aligned_M || row < m_actual) {\n      int idx = (int(tid.y) * M + m_base + row) * 3;\n      partials[idx + 0] = m_running[row];\n      partials[idx + 1] = s_running[row];\n      partials[idx + 2] = target_logit[row];\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n// Combine per-(v_block, row) partials into final lse[row] + loss_per_row[row].\n// Grid: ceil(M/TPG), TPG=128. Each thread owns one row and sequentially\n// log-add-exp-merges the grid_v slab partials with stable scaling. target is\n// a scalar per row so at most one slab captured a non-zero target_logit;\n// initial zero-init + sum recovers it.\n[[kernel]] void qcce_reduce_partials(\n    const device float* partials     [[buffer(0)]],\n    device float*       lse_out      [[buffer(1)]],\n    device float*       loss_per_row [[buffer(2)]],\n    const constant int& M            [[buffer(3)]],\n    const constant int& grid_v       [[buffer(4)]],\n    uint                gid          [[thread_position_in_grid]]) {\n  const int row = int(gid);\n  if (row >= M) return;\n\n  float m_acc = -INFINITY;\n  float s_acc = 0.0f;\n  float tgt_acc = 0.0f;\n\n  for (int v = 0; v < grid_v; v++) {\n    int idx = (v * M + row) * 3;\n    float m_p   = partials[idx + 0];\n    float s_p   = partials[idx + 1];\n    float tgt_p = partials[idx + 2];\n\n    float m_new = max(m_acc, m_p);\n    float scale_old = (m_acc > -INFINITY)\n        ? metal::fast::exp(m_acc - m_new) : 0.0f;\n    float scale_p = (m_p > -INFINITY)\n        ? metal::fast::exp(m_p - m_new) : 0.0f;\n    s_acc = s_acc * scale_old + s_p * scale_p;\n    m_acc = m_new;\n    tgt_acc += tgt_p;\n  }\n\n  float lse = metal::fast::log(s_acc) + m_acc;\n  lse_out[row] = lse;\n  loss_per_row[row] = lse - tgt_acc;\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Steel-based backward: hardware simdgroup_matrix FMA for both the Phase 1\n// logit recompute (X @ W^T) and the Phase 2 d_x accumulation (d_logit @ W).\n// Grid: (M/BM, V/V_slab). Each TG owns BM rows × one V-slab of V_slab v's,\n// walks the slab in BK-tile steps. For each v_tile:\n//   Phase 1: Steel MMA recomputes logits[BM, BN] (same kernel as forward).\n//   Phase 1b: convert logits to d_logit = (exp(logit-lse) - (v==tgt)) * cot/M,\n//             stored as T in TG memory [BM, BN_padded].\n//   Phase 2: for each k_tile in D/BN, a fresh QuantizedBlockLoader with\n//            reduction_dim=0 loads W[v_tile:v_tile+BK, k_tile:k_tile+BN],\n//            one BlockMMA step (K-dim = BK = v-axis, fully reduced in one\n//            call) produces dx_partial[BM, BN]; atomic_fetch_add flushes\n//            into the global fp32 d_x_acc[M, D].\n// Post-kernel: qcce_backward_finalize<T> casts fp32 accumulator to T.\n//\n// Requires M % BM == 0, V % BK == 0, D % BN == 0, V_slab % BK == 0.\n//\n// Locked params: BM=BN=BK=32, WM=WN=2 -> tgp_size=128 (4 simdgroups, same\n// layout as forward). Phase 1 MMA reuses the forward instantiation exactly;\n// Phase 2 MMA is a second instantiation with (transpose_b=false) since W's\n// fast axis in that phase is the N-axis (D-axis), not the K-axis.\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\ntemplate <\n    typename T,\n    int GS,\n    int BITS,\n    int BM,\n    int BN,\n    int BK,\n    int WM,\n    int WN,\n    bool aligned_M>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_backward_steel(\n    const device T*        cot          [[buffer(0)]],\n    const device T*        x            [[buffer(1)]],\n    const device uint32_t* w_packed     [[buffer(2)]],\n    const device T*        scales       [[buffer(3)]],\n    const device T*        biases       [[buffer(4)]],\n    const device int32_t*  targets      [[buffer(5)]],\n    const device float*    lse          [[buffer(6)]],\n    device atomic_float*   d_x_acc      [[buffer(7)]],\n    const constant int&    M            [[buffer(8)]],\n    const constant int&    D            [[buffer(9)]],\n    const constant int&    V            [[buffer(10)]],\n    const constant int&    V_slab       [[buffer(11)]],\n    uint3                  tid          [[threadgroup_position_in_grid]],\n    uint                   lid          [[thread_index_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   sg_id        [[simdgroup_index_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   lane         [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]]) {\n  constexpr int tgp_size   = WM * WN * 32;\n  constexpr int BK_padded  = BK + 16 / sizeof(T);\n  constexpr int BN_padded  = BN + 16 / sizeof(T);\n  constexpr int PACK       = 32 / BITS;\n  constexpr int BPP        = 4;\n\n  threadgroup T     Xs[BM * BK_padded];\n  threadgroup T     Ws_p1[BN * BK_padded];          // Phase 1: W[BN rows, BK cols]\n  threadgroup float logits_tile[BM * BN];\n  threadgroup T     d_logit_tile[BM * BN_padded];   // A matrix for Phase 2\n  threadgroup T     Ws_p2[BK * BN_padded];          // Phase 2: W[BK rows, BN cols]\n  threadgroup float dx_flush[BM * BN];\n  threadgroup float tg_lse[BM];\n  threadgroup int   tg_target[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_cot_over_M;\n\n  const int m_base = int(tid.x) * BM;\n  if (m_base >= M) return;\n  const int m_actual = aligned_M ? BM : min(BM, M - m_base);\n  const int v_slab_start = int(tid.y) * V_slab;\n  if (v_slab_start >= V) return;\n  const int v_slab_end = min(v_slab_start + V_slab, V);\n\n  if (lid < uint(BM)) {\n    bool in_range = aligned_M || int(lid) < m_actual;\n    tg_lse[lid]    = in_range ? lse[m_base + lid] : 0.0f;\n    tg_target[lid] = in_range ? targets[m_base + lid] : -1;\n  }\n  if (lid == 0) {\n    tg_cot_over_M = float(cot[0]) / float(M);\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Phase 1 MMA: logits[BM, BN] = X[BM, BK-loop] @ W[BN, BK-loop]^T\n  using mma_p1_t = mlx::steel::BlockMMA<\n      T, T, BM, BN, BK, WM, WN, false, true, BK_padded, BK_padded>;\n  using loader_x_t = mlx::steel::BlockLoader<\n      T, BM, BK, BK_padded, 1, tgp_size>;\n  using loader_w_p1_t = QuantizedBlockLoader<\n      T, BN, BK, BK_padded, 1, tgp_size, GS, BITS>;\n\n  // Phase 2 MMA: d_x[BM, BN] = d_logit[BM, BK] @ W[BK, BN]\n  // A tile = d_logit[BM, BN_padded] with K-dim = BK = BN (one-call reduction).\n  // B tile = Ws_p2[BK, BN_padded] with reduction_dim=0 (rows are v's).\n  using mma_p2_t = mlx::steel::BlockMMA<\n      T, T, BM, BN, BK, WM, WN, false, false, BN_padded, BN_padded>;\n  using loader_w_p2_t = QuantizedBlockLoader<\n      T, BK, BN, BN_padded, 0, tgp_size, GS, BITS>;\n\n  const int K_w = D * BPP / PACK;\n  const int K_g = D / GS;\n\n  for (int v_tile = v_slab_start; v_tile < v_slab_end; v_tile += BK) {\n    // === Phase 1: Steel MMA recompute of logits_tile[BM, BN] ===\n    const device T* x_ptr = x + m_base * (int64_t)D;\n    const device uint8_t* w_ptr_p1 =\n        ((const device uint8_t*)w_packed) + v_tile * (int64_t)K_w;\n    const device T* s_ptr_p1 = scales + v_tile * (int64_t)K_g;\n    const device T* b_ptr_p1 = biases + v_tile * (int64_t)K_g;\n\n    loader_x_t loader_x(x_ptr, D, Xs, sg_id, lane);\n    loader_w_p1_t loader_w_p1(w_ptr_p1, s_ptr_p1, b_ptr_p1, D, Ws_p1, sg_id, lane);\n    mma_p1_t mma_p1(sg_id, lane);\n    mma_p1.Ctile.clear();\n\n    for (int k = 0; k < D; k += BK) {\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n      if (aligned_M) {\n        loader_x.load_unsafe();\n      } else {\n        loader_x.load_safe(short2(BK, m_actual));\n      }\n      loader_w_p1.load_unsafe();\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n      mma_p1.mma(Xs, Ws_p1);\n      loader_x.next();\n      loader_w_p1.next();\n    }\n\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n    mma_p1.Ctile.template store<float, WM, WN, BN, 1>(\n        logits_tile + mma_p1.sm * BN + mma_p1.sn);\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    // === Phase 1b: logits -> d_logit (as T, padded leading dim) ===\n    for (int idx = int(lid); idx < BM * BN; idx += tgp_size) {\n      int r = idx / BN;\n      int c = idx - r * BN;\n      float logit = logits_tile[r * BN + c];\n      float p = metal::fast::exp(logit - tg_lse[r]);\n      int v_global = v_tile + c;\n      if (v_global == tg_target[r]) {\n        p -= 1.0f;\n      }\n      d_logit_tile[r * BN_padded + c] = T(p * tg_cot_over_M);\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    // === Phase 2: per-k_tile MMA + atomic-flush into d_x_acc ===\n    for (int k_tile = 0; k_tile < D; k_tile += BN) {\n      const device uint8_t* w_ptr_p2 =\n          ((const device uint8_t*)w_packed) + v_tile * (int64_t)K_w +\n          (k_tile * BPP) / PACK;\n      const device T* s_ptr_p2 = scales + v_tile * (int64_t)K_g + k_tile / GS;\n      const device T* b_ptr_p2 = biases + v_tile * (int64_t)K_g + k_tile / GS;\n\n      loader_w_p2_t loader_w_p2(\n          w_ptr_p2, s_ptr_p2, b_ptr_p2, D, Ws_p2, sg_id, lane);\n      mma_p2_t mma_p2(sg_id, lane);\n      mma_p2.Ctile.clear();\n\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n      loader_w_p2.load_unsafe();\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n      mma_p2.mma(d_logit_tile, Ws_p2);\n\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n      mma_p2.Ctile.template store<float, WM, WN, BN, 1>(\n          dx_flush + mma_p2.sm * BN + mma_p2.sn);\n      threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n      // Atomic-add dx_flush[BM, BN] -> d_x_acc[m_base..m_base+BM, k_tile..k_tile+BN]\n      for (int idx = int(lid); idx < BM * BN; idx += tgp_size) {\n        int r = idx / BN;\n        int c = idx - r * BN;\n        if (aligned_M || r < m_actual) {\n          atomic_fetch_add_explicit(\n              &d_x_acc[(m_base + r) * D + k_tile + c],\n              dx_flush[r * BN + c],\n              memory_order_relaxed);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n"

- "\n\nconstant constexpr int QCCE_THREADS = 128;\nconstant constexpr int QCCE_NUM_SGS = 4;\nconstant constexpr int QCCE_MAX_GROUPS = 64;  // upper bound on D / GS\n\ntemplate <typename T, int GS, int BM, int BITS>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_forward(\n    const device T*        x            [[buffer(0)]],\n    const device uint32_t* w_packed     [[buffer(1)]],\n    const device T*        scales       [[buffer(2)]],\n    const device T*        biases       [[buffer(3)]],\n    const device int32_t*  targets      [[buffer(4)]],\n    device float*          lse_out      [[buffer(5)]],\n    device float*          loss_per_row [[buffer(6)]],\n    const constant int&    M            [[buffer(7)]],\n    const constant int&    D            [[buffer(8)]],\n    const constant int&    V            [[buffer(9)]],\n    threadgroup T*         x_tile       [[threadgroup(0)]],\n    uint                   gid          [[threadgroup_position_in_grid]],\n    uint                   tid          [[thread_position_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   lane         [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]],\n    uint                   sg_id        [[simdgroup_index_in_threadgroup]]) {\n  const int m_base = int(gid) * BM;\n  if (m_base >= M) return;\n\n  constexpr int EL_PER_PACK = 32 / BITS;       // 8 for bits=4, 4 for bits=8\n  const int num_groups   = D / GS;\n  const int packs_per_row = D / EL_PER_PACK;\n  const int packs_per_grp = GS / EL_PER_PACK;\n\n  threadgroup int   tg_target[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_target_logit[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_sg_max[BM][QCCE_NUM_SGS];\n  threadgroup float tg_sg_sum[BM][QCCE_NUM_SGS];\n  threadgroup float x_sum_tg[BM][QCCE_MAX_GROUPS];\n\n  // Cooperative load: x[m_base..m_base+BM, :] -> x_tile[BM*D]\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * D; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / D;\n    const int k = idx - r * D;\n    x_tile[r * D + k] = x[(m_base + r) * D + k];\n  }\n  if (tid < BM) {\n    tg_target[tid] = targets[m_base + tid];\n    tg_target_logit[tid] = 0.0f;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Precompute x_sum[r][g] = sum over k in group g of x_tile[r, k].\n  // Each thread handles one (r, g) — only first BM*num_groups threads do work.\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * num_groups; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / num_groups;\n    const int g = idx - r * num_groups;\n    float xs = 0.0f;\n    const int k_start = g * GS;\n    for (int k = 0; k < GS; k++) {\n      xs += float(x_tile[r * D + k_start + k]);\n    }\n    x_sum_tg[r][g] = xs;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Per-thread, per-row online LSE state — all threads track identical values\n  // (they consume the same TG-broadcast m_tile/s_tile per iteration).\n  float m_running[BM];\n  float s_running[BM];\n  for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n    m_running[r] = -INFINITY;\n    s_running[r] = 0.0f;\n  }\n\n  const int num_tiles = (V + QCCE_THREADS - 1) / QCCE_THREADS;\n  for (int tile = 0; tile < num_tiles; tile++) {\n    const int v = tile * QCCE_THREADS + int(tid);\n    float logit[BM];\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = -INFINITY;\n\n    if (v < V) {\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = 0.0f;\n      const device uint32_t* w_row = w_packed + v * packs_per_row;\n      const device T* s_row_p = scales + v * num_groups;\n      const device T* b_row_p = biases + v * num_groups;\n\n      for (int g = 0; g < num_groups; g++) {\n        float s = float(s_row_p[g]);\n        float b = float(b_row_p[g]);\n        float qx_sum[BM];\n        for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) qx_sum[r] = 0.0f;\n        const int k0_g = g * GS;\n        for (int p = 0; p < packs_per_grp; p++) {\n          const int k0 = k0_g + p * EL_PER_PACK;\n          uint32_t packed = w_row[k0 / EL_PER_PACK];  // shared across BM rows\n          float qs[EL_PER_PACK];\n          if constexpr (BITS == 4) {\n            for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n              uint8_t byte = (packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff;\n              qs[byte_idx * 2]     = float(byte & 0x0f);\n              qs[byte_idx * 2 + 1] = float((byte >> 4) & 0x0f);\n            }\n          } else {  // BITS == 8\n            for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n              qs[byte_idx] = float((packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff);\n            }\n          }\n          for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n            for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n              qx_sum[r] += qs[i] * float(x_tile[r * D + k0 + i]);\n            }\n          }\n        }\n        for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n          logit[r] += s * qx_sum[r] + b * x_sum_tg[r][g];\n        }\n      }\n\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n        if (v == tg_target[r]) tg_target_logit[r] = logit[r];\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Per-row TG-wide max via 4-SG partial reduction.\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float sg_max = simd_max(logit[r]);\n      if (lane == 0) tg_sg_max[r][sg_id] = sg_max;\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    float new_m[BM];\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float m_tile = max(max(tg_sg_max[r][0], tg_sg_max[r][1]),\n                         max(tg_sg_max[r][2], tg_sg_max[r][3]));\n      new_m[r] = max(m_running[r], m_tile);\n    }\n\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float exp_term = (logit[r] > -INFINITY) ? metal::fast::exp(logit[r] - new_m[r]) : 0.0f;\n      float sg_sum = simd_sum(exp_term);\n      if (lane == 0) tg_sg_sum[r][sg_id] = sg_sum;\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float s_tile = tg_sg_sum[r][0] + tg_sg_sum[r][1] + tg_sg_sum[r][2] + tg_sg_sum[r][3];\n      float scale_old = (m_running[r] > -INFINITY) ? metal::fast::exp(m_running[r] - new_m[r]) : 0.0f;\n      s_running[r] = s_running[r] * scale_old + s_tile;\n      m_running[r] = new_m[r];\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (tid < BM) {\n    float lse = metal::fast::log(s_running[tid]) + m_running[tid];\n    lse_out[m_base + tid] = lse;\n    loss_per_row[m_base + tid] = lse - tg_target_logit[tid];\n  }\n}\n\n// Mean reduction: loss = mean(loss_per_row). One TG, 32 lanes (M is small).\ntemplate <typename T>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_loss_reduce(\n    const device float* loss_per_row [[buffer(0)]],\n    device T*           loss_out     [[buffer(1)]],\n    const constant int& M            [[buffer(2)]],\n    uint                lane         [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]]) {\n  float sum = 0.0f;\n  for (int i = int(lane); i < M; i += 32) {\n    sum += loss_per_row[i];\n  }\n  sum = simd_sum(sum);\n  if (lane == 0) {\n    loss_out[0] = T(sum / float(M));\n  }\n}\n\n// Backward: d_x[m, k] = sum_v (softmax[m, v] - 1{v==target[m]}) * cot/M * W[v, k]\n//\n// Two-phase per V-tile (128 v's per tile):\n//   Phase 1 (tid = v offset): recompute logit per row, derive d_logit per row,\n//     store in d_logit_tile[BM][128].\n//   Phase 2 (tid = k_chunk index): for each of 128 v's in this tile, dequant 8\n//     W values once and FMA into accum[BM][8]; flush into d_x_acc[BM][D]. The\n//     per-TG fp32 accumulator is exclusive across TGs (no atomics).\ntemplate <typename T, int GS, int BM, int BITS>\n[[kernel]] void qcce_backward(\n    const device T*        cot         [[buffer(0)]],\n    const device T*        x           [[buffer(1)]],\n    const device uint32_t* w_packed    [[buffer(2)]],\n    const device T*        scales      [[buffer(3)]],\n    const device T*        biases      [[buffer(4)]],\n    const device int32_t*  targets     [[buffer(5)]],\n    const device float*    lse         [[buffer(6)]],\n    device T*              d_x         [[buffer(7)]],\n    const constant int&    M           [[buffer(8)]],\n    const constant int&    D           [[buffer(9)]],\n    const constant int&    V           [[buffer(10)]],\n    threadgroup T*         x_tile      [[threadgroup(0)]],\n    threadgroup float*     d_x_acc     [[threadgroup(1)]],\n    uint                   gid         [[threadgroup_position_in_grid]],\n    uint                   tid         [[thread_position_in_threadgroup]],\n    uint                   lane        [[thread_index_in_simdgroup]],\n    uint                   sg_id       [[simdgroup_index_in_threadgroup]]) {\n  const int m_base = int(gid) * BM;\n  if (m_base >= M) return;\n\n  constexpr int EL_PER_PACK = 32 / BITS;\n  const int num_groups   = D / GS;\n  const int packs_per_row = D / EL_PER_PACK;\n  const int packs_per_grp = GS / EL_PER_PACK;\n\n  threadgroup int   tg_target[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_lse[BM];\n  threadgroup float tg_cot_over_M;\n  threadgroup float d_logit_tile[BM][QCCE_THREADS];\n  threadgroup float x_sum_tg[BM][QCCE_MAX_GROUPS];\n\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * D; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / D;\n    const int k = idx - r * D;\n    x_tile[r * D + k] = x[(m_base + r) * D + k];\n    d_x_acc[r * D + k] = 0.0f;\n  }\n  if (tid < BM) {\n    tg_target[tid] = targets[m_base + tid];\n    tg_lse[tid]    = lse[m_base + tid];\n  }\n  if (tid == 0) {\n    tg_cot_over_M = float(cot[0]) / float(M);\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  // Precompute x_sum[r][g] = sum over k in group g of x_tile[r, k].\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * num_groups; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / num_groups;\n    const int g = idx - r * num_groups;\n    float xs = 0.0f;\n    const int k_start = g * GS;\n    for (int k = 0; k < GS; k++) {\n      xs += float(x_tile[r * D + k_start + k]);\n    }\n    x_sum_tg[r][g] = xs;\n  }\n  threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n  const int num_tiles = (V + QCCE_THREADS - 1) / QCCE_THREADS;\n  for (int tile = 0; tile < num_tiles; tile++) {\n    const int v_base = tile * QCCE_THREADS;\n    const int v      = v_base + int(tid);\n\n    // Phase 1: recompute logit per row for this thread's v.\n    float logit[BM];\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = -INFINITY;\n\n    if (v < V) {\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) logit[r] = 0.0f;\n      const device uint32_t* w_row = w_packed + v * packs_per_row;\n      const device T* s_row_p = scales + v * num_groups;\n      const device T* b_row_p = biases + v * num_groups;\n\n      for (int g = 0; g < num_groups; g++) {\n        float s = float(s_row_p[g]);\n        float b = float(b_row_p[g]);\n        float qx_sum[BM];\n        for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) qx_sum[r] = 0.0f;\n        const int k0_g = g * GS;\n        for (int p = 0; p < packs_per_grp; p++) {\n          const int k0 = k0_g + p * EL_PER_PACK;\n          uint32_t packed = w_row[k0 / EL_PER_PACK];  // shared across BM rows\n          float qs[EL_PER_PACK];\n          if constexpr (BITS == 4) {\n            for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n              uint8_t byte = (packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff;\n              qs[byte_idx * 2]     = float(byte & 0x0f);\n              qs[byte_idx * 2 + 1] = float((byte >> 4) & 0x0f);\n            }\n          } else {  // BITS == 8\n            for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n              qs[byte_idx] = float((packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff);\n            }\n          }\n          for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n            for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n              qx_sum[r] += qs[i] * float(x_tile[r * D + k0 + i]);\n            }\n          }\n        }\n        for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n          logit[r] += s * qx_sum[r] + b * x_sum_tg[r][g];\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n      float p_val = 0.0f;\n      if (v < V) {\n        p_val = metal::fast::exp(logit[r] - tg_lse[r]);\n        if (v == tg_target[r]) p_val -= 1.0f;\n      }\n      d_logit_tile[r][tid] = p_val * tg_cot_over_M;\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n\n    // Phase 2: each thread handles k_chunks, accumulates over all 128 v's of\n    // this tile. W reads are shared across BM rows.\n    for (int k_chunk = int(tid); k_chunk < packs_per_row; k_chunk += QCCE_THREADS) {\n      const int k0 = k_chunk * EL_PER_PACK;\n      const int g  = k0 / GS;\n      float accum[BM][EL_PER_PACK];\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n        for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) accum[r][i] = 0.0f;\n      }\n\n      for (int vi = 0; vi < QCCE_THREADS; vi++) {\n        const int v_global = v_base + vi;\n        if (v_global >= V) break;\n        uint32_t packed = w_packed[v_global * packs_per_row + k_chunk];\n        float s = float(scales[v_global * num_groups + g]);\n        float b = float(biases[v_global * num_groups + g]);\n        float qs[EL_PER_PACK];\n        if constexpr (BITS == 4) {\n          for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n            uint8_t byte = (packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff;\n            qs[byte_idx * 2]     = float(byte & 0x0f);\n            qs[byte_idx * 2 + 1] = float((byte >> 4) & 0x0f);\n          }\n        } else {  // BITS == 8\n          for (int byte_idx = 0; byte_idx < 4; byte_idx++) {\n            qs[byte_idx] = float((packed >> (byte_idx * 8)) & 0xff);\n          }\n        }\n        for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n          float w_i = s * qs[i] + b;\n          for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n            float dl = d_logit_tile[r][vi];\n            accum[r][i] += dl * w_i;\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      for (int r = 0; r < BM; r++) {\n        for (int i = 0; i < EL_PER_PACK; i++) {\n          d_x_acc[r * D + k0 + i] += accum[r][i];\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    threadgroup_barrier(mem_flags::mem_threadgroup);\n  }\n\n  for (int idx = int(tid); idx < BM * D; idx += QCCE_THREADS) {\n    const int r = idx / D;\n    const int k = idx - r * D;\n    d_x[(m_base + r) * D + k] = T(d_x_acc[r * D + k]);\n  }\n}\n\n"
- "\n#include <cmath>\n#include <complex>\n#include <cstdint>\n#include <vector>\n#ifdef __ARM_FEATURE_FP16_SCALAR_ARITHMETIC\n#include <arm_fp16.h>\n#endif\nnamespace mlx::core {\nusing b.real();\n  if (imag != 0 && ((imag < 0) != (b.imag() < 0)))\n    imag += b.imag();\n  return {real, imag};\n}\ninline bool operator<=(const complex64_t& a, const complex64_t& b) {\n  return static_cast<complex64_t>(y); }\n}\nnamespace mlx::core::simd {\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nstruct Simd;\ntemplate <typename T>\nstatic constexpr int max_size = 1;\ntemplate <typename T>\nstruct Simd<T, 1> {\n  static constexpr int size = 1;\n  T value;\n  Simd() {}\n  template <typename U>\n  Simd(Simd<U, 1> v) : value(v.value) {}\n  template <typename U>\n  Simd(U v) : value(v) {}\n  T operator[](int) const {\n    return value;\n  }\n  T& operator[](int) {\n    return value;\n  }\n};\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nSimd<T, N> load(const T* x) {\n  return *(Simd<T, N>*)x;\n}\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nvoid store(T* dst, Simd<T, N> x) {\n  if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, bool> && N > 1) {\n    x = x & 1;\n  }\n  *(Simd<T, N>*)dst = x;\n}\ntemplate <typename, typename = void>\nconstexpr bool is_complex = false;\ntemplate <typename T>\nconstexpr bool is_complex<T, std::void_t<decltype(std::declval<T>().real())>> =\n    true;\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> rint(Simd<T, 1> in) {\n  if constexpr (is_complex<T>) {\n    return Simd<T, 1>{\n        T{std::rint(in.value.real()), std::rint(in.value.imag())}};\n  } else {\n    return Simd<T, 1>{std::rint(in.value)};\n  }\n}\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> rsqrt(Simd<T, 1> in) {\n  return T(1.0) / sqrt(in);\n}\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> recip(Simd<T, 1> in) {\n  return T(1.0) / in;\n}\ntemplate <typename T> Simd<T, 1> operator-(Simd<T, 1> in) { return std::negate{}(in.value); }\ntemplate <typename T> Simd<T, 1> operator!(Simd<T, 1> in) { return std::logical_not{}(in.value); }\ntemplate <typename T> Simd<T, 1> abs(Simd<T, 1> in) { return std::abs(in.value); }\ntemplate <typename T> Simd<T, 1> acos(Simd<T, 1> in) { return std::acos(in.value); }\ntemplate <typename T> }\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> log1p(Simd<T, 1> in) {\n  if constexpr (is_complex<T>) {\n    auto x = in.value.real();\n    auto y = in.value.imag();\n    auto zabs = std::abs(in.value);\n    auto theta = std::atan2(y, x + 1);\n    if (zabs < 0.5) {\n      auto r = x * (2 + x) + y * y;\n      if (r == 0) {\n        return Simd<T, 1>{T{x, theta}};\n      }\n      return Simd<T, 1>{T{((decltype(x))(0.5)) * std::log1p(r), theta}};\n    } else {\n      auto z0 = std::hypot(x + 1, y);\n      return Simd<T, 1>{T{std::log(z0), theta}};\n    }\n  } else {\n    return Simd<T, 1>{std::log1p(in.value)};\n  }\n}\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> log2(Simd<T, 1> in) {\n  if constexpr (is_complex<T>) {\n    auto out = std::log(in.value);\n    auto scale = decltype(out.real())(M_LN2);\n    return Simd<T, 1>{T{out.real() / scale, out.imag() / scale}};\n  } else {\n    return Simd<T, 1>{std::log2(in.value)};\n  }\n}\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> (!std::is_integral_v<T>) {\n    if (std::isnan(a)) {\n      return a;\n    }\n  }\n  return (a > b) ? a : b;\n}\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> minimum(Simd<T, 1> a_, Simd<T, 1> b_) {\n  T a = pow(Simd<T, 1> a, Simd<T, 1> b) {\n  T base = a.value;\n  T exp = b.value;\n  if constexpr (!std::is_integral_v<T>) {\n    return std::pow(base, exp);\n  } else {\n    T res = 1;\n    while (exp) {\n      if (exp & 1) {\n        res *= base;\n      }\n      exp >>= 1;\n      base *= base;\n    }\n    return res;\n  }\n}\ntemplate <typename T>\nSimd<T, 1> atan2(Simd<T, 1> a, Simd<T, 1> b) {\n  return std::atan2(a.value, b.value);\n}\ntemplate <typename T1, typename T2> Simd<bool, 1> operator >(Simd<T1, 1> a, Simd<T2, 1> b) { return a.value > b.value; } template <typename T1, typename T2> }\ntemplate <typename T> T min(Simd<T, 1> x) { return x.value; }\ntemplate <typename T> T sum(Simd<T, 1> x) { return x.value; }\ntemplate <typename T> T prod(Simd<T, 1> x) { return x.value; }\ntemplate <typename T> bool any(Simd<T, 1> x) { return x.value; }\ntemplate <typename T> bool all(Simd<T, 1> x) { return x.value; }\n}\n\nnamespace mlx::core::simd {\nconstexpr float inf = std::numeric_limits<float>::infinity();\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nSimd<T, N> exp(Simd<T, N> in) {\n  if constexpr (is_complex<T>) {\n    return Simd<T, 1>{std::exp(in.value)};\n  } else {\n    Simd<float, N> x_init = in;\n    auto x = x_init * 1.442695f;\n    Simd<float, N> ipart, fpart;\n    ipart = floor(x + 0.5);\n    fpart = x - ipart;\n    x = 1.535336188319500e-4f;\n    x = fma(x, fpart, 1.339887440266574e-3f);\n    x = fma(x, fpart, 9.618437357674640e-3f);\n    x = fma(x, fpart, 5.550332471162809e-2f);\n    x = fma(x, fpart, 2.402264791363012e-1f);\n    x = fma(x, fpart, 6.931472028550421e-1f);\n    x = fma(x, fpart, 1.000000000000000f);\n    Simd<int, N> epart = (Simd<int, N>(ipart) + 127) << 23;\n    auto result = select(isnan(x_init), x_init, (*(Simd<float, N>*)&epart) * x);\n    result = select(x_init > 88.0f, Simd<float, N>(inf), result);\n    result = select(x_init < -88.0f, Simd<float, N>(0), result);\n    return Simd<T, N>(result);\n  }\n}\ntemplate <bool Sine, typename T, int N>\nSimd<T, N> sincos(Simd<T, N> in) {\n  auto sign_mask_sin = in < 0;\n  in = abs(in);\n  Simd<float, N> x = in;\n  auto y = x * 1.27323954473516f;\n  Simd<uint32_t, N> emm2 = y;\n  emm2 = emm2 + 1;\n  emm2 = emm2 & ~1;\n  y = emm2;\n  auto poly_mask = (emm2 & 2) != 0;\n  x = fma(y, Simd<float, N>(-0.78515625f), x);\n  x = fma(y, Simd<float, N>(-2.4187564849853515625e-4f), x);\n  x = fma(y, Simd<float, N>(-3.77489497744594108e-8f), x);\n  sign_mask_sin = sign_mask_sin ^ ((emm2 & 4) != 0);\n  auto sign_mask_cos = ((emm2 - 2) & 4) != 0;\n  auto z = x * x;\n  auto y1 =\n      fma(z, Simd<float, N>(2.443315711809948e-5f), -1.388731625493765e-3f);\n  auto y2 = fma(z, Simd<float, N>(-1.9515295891e-4f), 8.3321608736e-3f);\n  y1 = fma(y1, z, 4.166664568298827e-2f);\n  y2 = fma(y2, z, -1.6666654611e-1f);\n  y1 = y1 * z;\n  y2 = y2 * z;\n  y1 = y1 * z;\n  y2 = fma(x, y2, x);\n  y1 = fma(z, Simd<float, N>(-0.5f), y1);\n  y1 = y1 + 1.0f;\n  if constexpr (Sine) {\n    auto ys = select(poly_mask, y1, y2);\n    return select(sign_mask_sin, -ys, ys);\n  } else {\n    auto yc = select(poly_mask, y2, y1);\n    return select(sign_mask_cos, yc, -yc);\n  }\n}\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nSimd<T, N> sin(Simd<T, N> x) {\n  if constexpr (is_complex<T>) {\n    return std::sin(x.value);\n  } else {\n    return sincos<true>(x);\n  }\n}\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nSimd<T, N> cos(Simd<T, N> x) {\n  if constexpr (is_complex<T>) {\n    return std::cos(x.value);\n  } else {\n    return sincos<false>(x);\n  }\n}\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nSimd<T, N> erf(Simd<T, N> x) {\n  Simd<float, N> v = x;\n  auto t = recip(fma(Simd<float, N>(0.3275911f), abs(v), 1.0f));\n  auto r = fma(Simd<float, N>(1.061405429f), t, -1.453152027f);\n  r = fma(r, t, 1.421413741f);\n  r = fma(r, t, -0.284496736f);\n  r = fma(r, t, 0.254829592f);\n  auto e = -exp(-v * v);\n  auto result = Simd<T, N>(fma(e * t, r, 1.0f));\n  return select(x > 0, result, -result);\n}\ntemplate <typename T, int N>\nSimd<T, N> erfinv(Simd<T, N> a_) {\n  Simd<float, N> a = a_;\n  auto t = fma(a, 0.0f - a, 1.0f);\n  t = log(t);\n  auto lhs = [](auto t) {\n    Simd<float, N> p;\n    p = 3.03697567e-10f;\n    p = fma(p, t, 2.93243101e-8f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 1.22150334e-6f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 2.84108955e-5f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 3.93552968e-4f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 3.02698812e-3f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 4.83185798e-3f);\n    p = fma(p, t, -2.64646143e-1f);\n    return fma(p, t, 8.40016484e-1f);\n  };\n  auto rhs = [](auto t) {\n    Simd<float, N> p;\n    p = 5.43877832e-9f;\n    p = fma(p, t, 1.43285448e-7f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 1.22774793e-6f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 1.12963626e-7f);\n    p = fma(p, t, -5.61530760e-5f);\n    p = fma(p, t, -1.47697632e-4f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 2.31468678e-3f);\n    p = fma(p, t, 1.15392581e-2f);\n    p = fma(p, t, -2.32015476e-1f);\n    return fma(p, t, 8.86226892e-1f);\n  };\n  auto thresh = 6.125f;\n  if constexpr (N == 1) {\n    if ((abs(t) > thresh).value) {\n      return a * lhs(t);\n    } else {\n      return a * rhs(t);\n    }\n  } else {\n    return a * select(abs(t) > thresh, lhs(t), rhs(t));\n  }\n}\n}\n\nnamespace mlx::core::detail {\nusing namespace mlx::core::simd;\nstruct Abs { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x) { return simd::abs(x); } template <typename T> operator()(T x) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x)).value; }\n};\nstruct Sigmoid {\n  template <int N, typename T>\n  Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x) {\n    auto y = 1.0f / (1.0f + simd::exp(simd::abs(x)));\n    return simd::select(x < Simd<T, N>{0}, y, Simd<T, N>{1} - y);\n  }\n  template <typename T> T operator()(T x) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x)).value; }\n};\nstruct Sign {\n  template <int N, typename T>\n  Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x) {\n    auto z = Simd<T, N>{0};\n    auto o = Simd<T, N>{1};\n    auto m = Simd<T, N>{-1};\n    if constexpr (std::is_unsigned_v<T>) {\n      return simd::select(x == z, z, o);\n    } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, complex64_t>) {\n      return simd::select(x == z, x, Simd<T, N>(x / simd::abs(x)));\n    } else {\n      return simd::select(x < z, m, simd::select(x > z, o, z));\n    }\n  }\n  template <typename T> T operator()(T x) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x)).value; }\n};\nstruct Square {\n  template <int N, typename T>\n  Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x) {\n    return x * x;\n  }\n  template <typename T> T operator()(T x) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x)).value; }\n};\ntemplate <int N>\nSimd<float, N> fp32_from_bits(Simd<uint32_t, N> x) {\n  return *(Simd<float, N>*)(&x);\n}\ntemplate <int N>\nSimd<uint32_t, N> fp32_to_bits(Simd<float, N> x) {\n  return *(Simd<uint32_t, N>*)(&x);\n}\nstruct ToFP8 {\n  template <typename T, int N>\n  Simd<uint8_t, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> f) {\n    uint32_t fp8_max = 543 << 21;\n    auto denorm_mask = Simd<uint32_t, N>(141 << 23);\n    Simd<uint32_t, N> f_bits;\n    Simd<float, N> f32 = f;\n    f_bits = fp32_to_bits(f32);\n    Simd<uint8_t, N> result = 0u;\n    auto sign = f_bits & 0x80000000;\n    f_bits = f_bits ^ sign;\n    auto f_bits_low =\n        fp32_to_bits(fp32_from_bits(f_bits) + fp32_from_bits(denorm_mask));\n    auto result_low = Simd<uint8_t, N>(f_bits_low - denorm_mask);\n    auto mant_odd = Simd<uint8_t, N>((f_bits >> 20) & 1);\n    auto f_bits_high = f_bits + (((uint32_t)(7 - 127) << 23) + 0x7FFFF);\n    f_bits_high = f_bits_high + Simd<uint32_t, N>(mant_odd);\n    auto result_high = Simd<uint8_t, N>(f_bits_high >> 20);\n    result = select(f_bits < (121 << 23), result_low, result_high);\n    auto result_sat = Simd<uint8_t, N>(0x7E);\n    result = select(f_bits >= fp8_max, result_sat, result);\n    return result | Simd<uint8_t, N>(sign >> 24);\n  }\n  template <typename T>\n  uint8_t operator()(T x) {\n    return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x)).value;\n  }\n};\nstruct FromFP8 {\n  template <int N>\n  Simd<float, N> operator()(Simd<uint8_t, N> x) {\n    auto v = Simd<uint16_t, N>(x & 127) << 7;\n    Simd<float, N> out;\n    if constexpr (simd::max_size<float16_t> >= N) {\n      auto converted = *(Simd<float16_t, N>*)(&v);\n      out = converted * 256.0;\n    } else {\n      for (int i = 0; i < N; ++i) {\n        auto converted = *(float16_t*)(&v[i]);\n        out[i] = converted * 256.0;\n      }\n    }\n    auto sign = Simd<bool, N>(x & 128);\n    return select(sign, -out, out);\n  }\n  float operator()(uint8_t x) {\n    return (*this)(Simd<uint8_t, 1>(x)).value;\n  }\n};\n}\nnamespace mlx::core::detail {\nusing namespace mlx::core::simd;\nstruct Add { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator+(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct ArcTan2 { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return atan2(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct Divide { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator/(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct Multiply { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator*(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct Subtract { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator-(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct LogicalAnd { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator&&(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct LogicalOr { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator||(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct BitwiseAnd { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator&(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct BitwiseOr { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator|(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, 1>(x), Simd<T, 1>(y)).value; } };\nstruct BitwiseXor { template };\nstruct LeftShift { template <int N, typename T> Simd<T, N> operator()(Simd<T, N> x, Simd<T, N> y) { return operator<<(x, y); } template <typename T> T operator()(T x, T y) { return (*this)(Simd<T, N> y) {\n    auto maxval = maximum(x, y);\n    auto minval = minimum(x, y);\n    auto mask = minval == -inf || maxval == inf;\n    auto out = maxval + log1p(exp(minval - maxval));\n    return
